- $\log(|v| + 1)$ — a logarithmic term in v
- $\sin(v)$ — a sinusoidal term in v
- $v \cdot x^2$ — a cross term
- $v$ — linear term

These terms ($\log(|v|+1)$ and $\sin(v)$) are highly nonlinear and cannot be represented by polynomials in v (like $v^2$, $v^3$, $v \cdot |v|$), exponentials ($\exp(cv^2)$), or simple algebraic combinations.

- Exponential terms in v ($\exp(cv^2)$)
- $\sin(t)$ or $\cos(t)$ (not $\sin(v)$)
- Various functions of x

No candidate contains either $\log(|v| + \text{const})$ or $\sin(v)$, so none can match the GT exactly.
